5.13.2 POST /api/hccgw/webhook/v1/config/save
Save message push configurations.

Notes
● Currently, only one Webhook configuration is allowed per account.
● Callback push URLs must use HTTPS protocol.
● After the retry attempts reached the limit, messages will be discarded and persisted for 1 month.

  Integrators can contact technical support to re-push the valid messages.
● Refer to Webhook Message Push for the detailed process of secret key signature configurations.



Request URL
https://{areaDomain}/api/hccgw/webhook/v1/config/save




                                                            245
Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide


Request Parameters

                                           Table 5-101 Request Header
            Parameter                Req. or Opt.    Data Type                   Description
    Content-Type                    Req.            String       Data format. Only "application/​json" is
                                                                 supported.
    Token                           Req.            String       Token. The maximum length is 64.

                                            Table 5-102 Request Body
            Parameter                Req. or Opt.    Data Type                   Description
    callbackUrl                     Req.            String       Callback push address (must support both
                                                                 GET and POST requests, and require
                                                                 HTTPS protocol). The maximum length is
                                                                 256 characters.
    retryTimes                      Opt.            Integer      Retry attempts. Range: [-1,5]. Default: 3.
                                                                 The value -1 indicates unlimited retries
                                                                 within 2 hours.
    retryDelay                      Opt.            Long         Retry interval (millisecond).
    signSecret                      Opt.            String       Secret key configuration for signatures
                                                                 (used for signing pushed information).
                                                                 Defaults to SecretKey (SK) if it is empty.
                                                                 The length is from 8 to 32 characters.
                                                                 Format: A combination of letters and
                                                                 digits.

Request Example
{
     "callbackUrl": "https://xxx.com",
     "retryTimes": 3,
     "retryDelay": 1000,
     "signSecret": "xxxx"
}




                                                           246
Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide


Response Parameters

              Parameter       Req. or Opt.    Data Type                 Description
    errorCode                Req.            String       Response status or error code: 0-
                                                          succeeded, other codes-failed (refer
                                                          to Status and Error Code for details).
                                                          Each code can contain up to 32
                                                          characters.

Response Example

     "errorCode": "0"

5.14.7 POST /api/hccgw/acspm/v1/access/level/delete
Batch delete access levels.

      Note
● If the access level ID list in the request contains non-existent or deleted access level IDs, the API

  call result remains unaffected.
● If the field accessLevelIdList is absent or empty, all levels will be deleted.




Request URL
https://{areaDomain}/api/hccgw/acspm/v1/access/level/delete
Request Parameters

                                         Table 5-118 Request Header
             Parameter           Req. or Opt.    Data Type                    Description
    Token                        Req.           String        Token. The maximum length is 64.
    Content-Type                 Req.           String        Data format. Only "application/​json" is
                                                              supported.




                                                      261
Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide


                                              Table 5-119 Request Body
             Parameter              Req. or Opt.      Data Type                      Description
    accessLevelIdList              Req.              String[]       List of access levels to be delete.

                                                                          Note
                                                                    If this field is empty, all access levels will
                                                                    be deleted.

Request Example
{
     "accessLevelIdList": ["access_level_001","access_level_002"]
}

Response Parameters

              Parameter                 Req. or Opt.      Data Type                    Description
    errorCode                          Req.              String        Response status or error code: 0-
                                                                       succeeded, other codes-failed (refer
                                                                       to Status and Error Code for details).
                                                                       Each code can contain up to 32
                                                                       characters.
    message                            Opt.              String        Status or error description.
    data                               Req.              Object        Data returned when the request
                                                                       succeeded.
    -accessLevelFailedList             Req.              Object[]      Failed access level list.
    --id                               Req.              string        Failed access level ID.
    --name                             Req.              string        Failed access level name.
    --errorCode                        Req.              string        Error code of failed deletion.

Response Example
{
     "errorCode": "0",
     "data": {
       "accessLevelFailedList": [
         {
           "id": "res_001",
           "name": "res_001",
           "errorCode": "LAP000100"




                                                           262
Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide

            }
        ]
    }
}

Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide

A.2 Time/Date Format

A.2.1 ISO 8601 Time Format Instruction
ISO 8601, Data Elements and Interchange Formats–Information Interchange–Representation of
Dates and Times, is an international standard covering the exchange of date and time-related data
format issued by ISO. An uppercase T should be added before an exact time to represent the
combination of date and time. Beijing time 5:30:08 PM May 3rd, 2004 can be written as
2004-05-03T17:30:08+08:00 or 20040503T173008+08.


A.2.2 Date Format Type

                    Format                                          Description
yyyy/MM/dd                                       yyyy, the year of 4 digits containing era.
                                                 MM, the month of 2 digits. The number zero is
                                                 added to months of only one digit.
                                                 dd, the date of a month. The number zero is
                                                 added to dates of only one digit.
                                                 E.g., 2024/01/31
yyyy-MM-dd                                       E.g., 2024-01-31
yyyy.MM.dd                                       E.g., 2024.01.31
dd/MM/yyyy                                       E.g., 31/01/2024
dd-MM-yyyy                                       E.g., 31-01-2024
MM-dd-yyyy                                       E.g., 01-31-2024
yy-MM-dd                                         yy, the year of 2 digits without era. The number
                                                 zero is added to years of only one digit.
                                                 E.g., 24-01-31
yy/MM/dd                                         E.g., 24/01/31
dd/MM/yy                                         E.g., 24.01.31
yy.MM.dd                                         E.g., 24.01.31
yyyyddMM                                         E.g., 20243101
yyyyMMdd                                         E.g., 20240131
MMddyyyy                                         E.g., 01312024




                                               306
Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide



                Format                                   Description
ddMMyyyy                             E.g., 31012024
yyddMM                               E.g., 243101
yyMMdd                               E.g., 240131
MMddyy                               E.g., 013124
ddMMyy                               E.g., 310124


A.2.3 Time Format Type

                Format                                   Description
HH:mm                                HH, the hour in 24-hour format. The number
                                     zero is added to hours and minutes of only one
                                     digit.
                                     E.g., 13:30, 01:30
h:mm                                 h, the hour in 12-hour format. No zero is added
                                     to hours of only one digit.
                                     E.g., 1:30
hh:mm tt                             tt, the indicator of AM/PM.
                                     hh, the hour in 12-hour format. The number
                                     zero is added to hours of only one digit.
                                     E.g., 01:30 AM
h:mm tt                              E.g., 1:30 AM
HH:mm:ss                             ss, the second. The number zero is added to
                                     seconds of only one digit.
                                     E.g., 01:30:05
h:mm:ss                              E.g., 1:30:05
hh:mm:ss tt                          E.g., 01:30:05 AM
h:mm:ss tt                           E.g., 1:30:05 AM
HHmm                                 E.g., 1330
Hmm                                  H, the hour in 24-hour format. No zero is added
                                     to hours of only one digit.
                                     E.g., 130




                                   307
Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide



                     Format                                              Description
HHmmss                                               E.g., 013005
hmmss                                                E.g., 13005


A.2.4 Time Duration Format Type

                     Format                                              Description
HH:MM                                                Duration in hour and minute.
                                                     E.g., 01:30
MM                                                   Duration in minute.
                                                     E.g., 120

                                                            is 64.

A.3.20 AlarmMsg
The table here shows the information of an alarm event..


  Parameter Name           Data Type                                 Description
guid                 String                 GUID.
dataRetransmission Integer                  Whether it is real-​time alarm: 0-alarm uploaded via
                                            ANR, 1-alarm uploaded in real-​time.
msgType              String                 Alarm message type: "0" (end message), "1" (start
                                            message, or pulse, repeated GUID means pulse), "2"
                                            (confirm message), "3" (mark message).
alarmState           String                 Whether the alarm is in start status: "1" (start), "0"
                                            (end).
pulseAlarm           String                 Whether the alarm is pulse alarm: "0" (non-pulse
                                            alarm), "1" (pulse alarm).
alarmMainCategory String                    Alarm main category.
alarmSubCategory     String                 Alarm sub category.
timeInfo             AlarmTimeInfo          Alarm time.
eventSource          AlarmEventSource       Alarm event source.
alarmRule            AlarmRule              Alarm rule.
alarmPriority        AlarmPriority          Alarm priority.
markState            String                 Whether the alarm is tagged: "0" (untagged), "1"
                                            (tagged).
affirmedState        String                 Whether the alarm is acknowledged: "0"
                                            (unacknowledged), "1" (acknowledged).
fileInfo             AlarmFileInfo          Alarm file details.




                                                  316
Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide



  Parameter Name             Data Type                                Description
linkageType          String[]                  Linkage type: "0"-recording linkage, "1"-GIS map
                                               linkage, "2"-alarm output linkage, "3"-pop-up window
                                               linkage, "4"-door linkage.
linkageConfig        AlarmLinkageConfig Linkage configuration.
vehicleRelatedInfo   VehicleRelatedInfo        Linked vehicle information.
queueRelatedInfo     QueueRelatedInfo          Queuing-alarm related information.
anprInfo             ANPRInfo                  Vehicle blocklist/allowlist alarm event details.

                                                    control device), 2005 (alarm device), 2008
                                                    (video intercom), 2010 (data communication
                                                    device), 2020 (broadcast), 2021 (on-board
                                                    device), 2031 (cloud storage box);
                                                    Logical resource: 1001 (camera), 1002 (door),
                                                    1003 (zone).

offlineDuration               long                  Offline duration (unit: ms).

     Parameter      Req. or    Data Type                          Description
       Name          Opt.
ID                Req.         String      Alarm priority ID, which consists of up to 64 characters.
level             Opt.         String      Alarm priority level, which contains level 1 (the highest
                                           level), 2, and 3. It consists of up to 64 characters.
levelName         Opt.         String      Level name, which consists of up to 64 characters.
color             Opt.         String      Alarm priority level color, which is the value of RGB, for
                                           example: #F40B0B. It consists of up to 64 characters.

A.4 Status and Error Code

Internal Errors

           Error Code                     Error Description                 Debug Suggestion
CCF000001                           Parameter error.                Compare documents to check if the
                                                                    parameter is correct.
CCF000004                           Database operation failed.      Check the database operation.
CCF000005                           No permission to operate        Check your permissions.
                                    this resource.
CCF000007                           Internal calling failed.        Check request parameters
                                                                    according to the error message.
CCF038002                           Name length exceeded            Adjust name length.
                                    limit.
CCF038005                           Name cannot contain             Remove special characters.
                                    special characters.
CCF038007                           User is not assigned with       Contact the platform to check
                                    the access level.               person's access level.
CCF038009                           Person group does not           Person group does not exist.
                                    exist.




                                                   380
Hik-Connect for Teams (HikCentral Connect) OpenAPI V2.15.0 Developer Guide



        Error Code            Error Description                Debug Suggestion
CCF038014                Invalid first name of         Check and edit the first name of
                         person.                       person.
CCF038015                Invalid family name of        Check and edit the family name of
                         person.                       person.
CCF038016                Invalid person ID.            Check the person's personCode.
CCF038017                Invalid person's full name.   Check the person's full name.
CCF038019                Invalid person email.         Check the email.
CCF038020                Invalid person's phone No.    Check the phone No.
CCF038021                Invalid person's              Check the person's description.
                         description.
CCF038022                Invalid person's validity.    Check the person's validity.
CCF038023                Person does not exist.        Person does not exist.
CCF038024                Person ID already exists.     Check the person 's personCode.
CCF038025                Person ID does not exist.     Check the person 's personCode.
CCF038026                Person's picture does not     Check the person's picture.
                         exist.
CCF038028                Saving the person's picture Check if the picture information is
                         failed.                     correct.
CCF038029                No more persons are           Check the number of added
                         allowed.                      persons (free:100, fee-paying:
                                                       50,000.
CCF038031                Adding person failed.         Check all information of added
